Patterns Across Go Repositories\\n\\n### Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n\\nKubernetes implements exponential backoff through multiple layered components:\\n\\n**Core Implementation:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/wait/backoff.go`: Contains the primary `ExponentialBackoff(backoff Backoff, condition ConditionFunc)` function which implements the wait-retry pattern. It decays through backoff.Steps with exponentially increasing wait durations using `backoff.Step()`. Also provides `ExponentialBackoffWithContext()` for context-aware cancellation.\\n- `pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff/exponential_backoff.go`: Defines the `ExponentialBackoff` struct with `SafeToRetry()`, `Update()`, and `NewExponentialBackoffError()` methods. Uses initial duration of 500ms, doubling up to 2m2s max.\\n\\n**Client Retry Wrapper:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/retry/util.go`: The `OnError()` function wraps `wait.ExponentialBackoff()` to retry functions on specific retriable errors using the conflict-safe `DefaultRetry` backoff config (5 steps, 1s initial, 1.5x factor).\\n\\n**Webhook Integration:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/webhook.go`: Implements `WithExponentialBackoff()` function for webhook retry (up to 5 attempts). Provides `DefaultRetryBackoffWithInitialDelay()` for custom webhook backoff configuration.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/authenticator/token/webhook/webhook.go`: Uses `DefaultRetryBackoff()` for token review webhook retries.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go`: Creates audit webhook backend with configurable `retryBackoff`.\\n\\n**Component Usage:**\\n- `pkg/util/goroutinemap/goroutinemap.go`: GoRoutineMap uses exponentialbackoff.ExponentialBackoff for operation-level backoff tracking.\\n- `pkg/volume/util/nestedpendingoperations/nestedpendingoperations.go`: NestedPendingOperations uses exponentialbackoff.ExponentialBackoff in operation struct.\\n- `test/utils/create_resources.go`: Test helper `RetryWithExponentialBackOff()` uses wait.ExponentialBackoff with fixed parameters (100ms, 3x factor, 0 jitter, 6 steps).\\n- `pkg/kubelet/watchdog/watchdog_linux.go`: Uses `wait.ExponentialBackoffWithContext()` for watchdog systemd notification.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/nodeshutdown/nodeshutdown_manager_linux.go`: Uses `wait.ExponentialBackoff()` to reload login configuration.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go`: CSI plugin initialization uses exponential backoff (30ms initial, 1.5x factor).\\n\\n**Rate Limiting:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/default_rate_limiters.go`: Defines `TypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter` for work queue rate limiting with exponential backoff.\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\nGrafana uses multiple exponential backoff implementations across different services:\\n\\n**Git Repository Retry:**\\n- `apps/provisioning/pkg/repository/git/repository.go`: Imports `github.com/grafana/nanogit/retry` (external library) and uses `retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier` via `defaultGitRetrier()` with 8 max attempts (1 initial + 7 retries), 100ms initial delay, capped at 5 seconds. Integrates via `ensureRetryContext()` and `retry.FromContext()`/`retry.ToContext()`.\\n\\n**Alert Scheduling:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/retry.go`: Implements `newExponentialBackoffRetryer()` wrapping `backoff.BackOff` from cenkalti/backoff library with max retries, initial/max delays, and randomization factor.\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/recording_rule.go`: Uses the exponential backoff retrier for recording rule execution.\\n\\n**Resource Provisioning:**\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/resources/retry_client.go`: Wraps dynamic.ResourceInterface with `retryWithBackoff()` using Kubernetes' `wait.ExponentialBackoff` (100ms initial, 2x factor, 0.1 jitter, 8 steps, 5s cap). Test at line 431 validates exponential backoff calculation.\\n\\n**Generic Retry Helper:**\\n- `pkg/util/retryer/retryer.go`: Provides `Retry()` function with manual exponential backoff calculation: `delay := minDelay * time.Duration(1<<attempt)`.
